<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хвалить.html>хвали́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">xvalítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хвалиться.html>хвали́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">xvalítʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:похвалиться.html>похвали́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to brag, to boast <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">+ instrumental of thing boasted about</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li>to take credit for</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to be praised for (something)</li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хвалить.html>хвали́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">xvalítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

<h4><span id=".D0.A1.D0.B8.D0.BD.D0.BE.D0.BD.D0.B8.D0.BC.D1.8B"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Синонимы"><a href = vnd.unilang:синоним.html>Сино́нимы</a></span></h4>

***хватать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:хватать.html>хвата́ть</a> (640)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Inherited from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">хватати</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">xvatati</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*xvatati</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хватать.html>хвата́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">xvatátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:схватить.html>схвати́ть</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хватить.html>хвати́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to grasp, to grab, to seize, to snap, to snatch, to catch, to catch hold of
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:хватать.html>хвата́ть</a></b> кого́-либо <a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:рука.html>ру́ку</a>/<a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:рука.html>ру́ку</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>xvatátʹ</b> kovó-libo zá ruku/za rúku</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to seize / grasp smb. by the hand</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:хватать.html>хвата́ть</a></b> что́-либо <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:лето.html>лету́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>xvatátʹ</b> štó-libo na letú</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to be very quick at something.</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:хватать.html>хвата́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>что</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:попасть.html>попа́ло</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>xvatátʹ</b> što popálo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to seize up whatever comes to hand</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:хватать.html>хвата́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:душа.html>душу</a>/<a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:душа.html>ду́шу</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>xvatátʹ</b> zá dušu/za dúšu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to tug at one's heart-strings</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>In this meaning, the alternative perfective <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хватить.html>хвати́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">xvatítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> is low colloquial.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_2">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хватать.html>хвата́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">xvatátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хватить.html>хвати́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">impersonal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to suffice, to be enough, to be sufficient, to adequate
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>мне</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ты.html>тебя́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:хватать.html>хвата́ет</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">mne tebjá ne <b>xvatájet</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">I miss you.</span> (literally, “<span class="e-literally">there is not enough of you for me</span>”)</div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́того</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:хватить.html>хва́тит</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">étovo <b>xvátit</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">this will be sufficient / enough</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сегодня.html>сего́дня</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:хватить.html>хва́тит</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">na sevódnja <b>xvátit</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">that'll do for today!; let's call it a day</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>у</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>него́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:хватить.html>хвати́ло</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:мужество.html>му́жества</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:делать.html>де́лать</a> что́-ли́бо)</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">u nevó <b>xvatílo</b> múžestva (délatʹ štó-líbo)</i> ― <span class="e-translation">he had the courage (to do something)</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>ему́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:хватить.html>хвати́ло</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:время.html>вре́мени</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:делать.html>де́лать</a> что́-ли́бо)</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">jemú <b>xvatílo</b> vrémeni (délatʹ štó-líbo)</i> ― <span class="e-translation">he had (the) time enough</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́того</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:должный.html>должно́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:хватить.html>хвати́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:зима.html>зи́му</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">étovo dolžnó <b>xvatítʹ</b> ná zimu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">this must last the winter</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́того</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>ему́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:хватить.html>хва́тит</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:месяц.html>ме́сяц</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">étovo jemú <b>xvátit</b> na mésjac</i> ― <span class="e-translation">it will last him a month</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>мне</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:хватить.html>хва́тит</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">mne <b>xvátit</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">that's enough for me, that will do for me</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:хватить.html>хва́тит</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">ne <b>xvátit</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">not be enough</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:хватать.html>хвата́ет</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:время.html>вре́мени</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:для.html>для</a> кого́-ли́бо / чего́-ли́бо; <a href = vnd.unilang:делать.html>де́лать</a> что-ли́бо)</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">ne <b>xvatájet</b> vrémeni (dlja kovó-líbo / čevó-líbo; délatʹ što-líbo)</i> ― <span class="e-translation">there isn't enough time (for something; to do something)</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>у</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>него́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:хватать.html>хвата́ет</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:время.html>вре́мени</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">u nevó ne <b>xvatájet</b> vrémeni</i> ― <span class="e-translation">he is hard pressed for time</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>у</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>него́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:хватать.html>хвата́ет</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:деньги.html>де́нег</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">u nevó ne <b>xvatájet</b> déneg</i> ― <span class="e-translation">he is short of money</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>у</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>него́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:шарик.html>ша́риков</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:хватать.html>хвата́ет</a></b></i> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">u nevó šárikov ne <b>xvatájet</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">he is not all there</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>ему́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:порох.html>по́роха</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:хватать.html>хвата́ет</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">jemú póroxa ne <b>xvatájet</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">he lacks the energy; he has not got it in him, he is not up to it</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>(<i>idiomatic expressions</i>)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:хватить.html>хва́тит</a></b>!</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>xvátit</b>!</i> ― <span class="e-translation">that will do!; enough of that!, enough!, stop it!</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>меня́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:хватить.html>хва́тит</a></b>!</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">s menjá <b>xvátit</b>!</i> ― <span class="e-translation">I have had enough!</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́того</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:еще.html>ещё</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:хватать.html>хвата́ло</a></b></i> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">étovo ješčó ne <b>xvatálo</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">that's a bit too thick, that's the limit, that would be the last straw</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***хвататься.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:хвататься.html>хвата́ться</a> (5250)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хватать.html>хвата́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">xvatátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хвататься.html>хвата́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">xvatátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хватиться.html>хвати́ться</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:схватиться.html>схвати́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to snatch <i>(at)</i>, to grip, to pluck <i>(at)</i>, to catch <i>(at)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:хвататься.html>хвата́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:соломинка.html>соло́минку</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>xvatátʹsja</b> za solóminku</i> ― <span class="e-translation">catch at a straw; clutch at straws</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to take up
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:столько.html>сто́лько</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:дело.html>де́л</a> - <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:знать.html>зна́ешь</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>что</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:хвататься.html>хвата́ться</a></b></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">stólʹko del - ne znáješʹ za što <b>xvatátʹsja</b></i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">there are so many things to do, you don't know what to start with</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хватать.html>хвата́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">xvatátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

***хватить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:хватить.html>хвати́ть</a> (659)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хватить.html>хвати́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">xvatítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хватать.html>хвата́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to snatch and devour <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of animals</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to gulp down (liquid)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial<span class="ib-comma">,</span> intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to get drunk</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to finagle</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to endure (something unpleasant)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to go too far in, to get carried away in (statements or plans)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to hit hard, to punch</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to break by striking, to shatter</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to strike (someone) <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of a heart attack, paralysis, etc.</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to strike, to manifest suddenly <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of rain, frost, wind, etc.</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial<span class="ib-comma">,</span> impersonal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to damage
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">овсы́ <b><a href = vnd.unilang:хватить.html>хвати́ло</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:град.html>гра́дом</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">ovsý <b>xvatílo</b> grádom</i> ― <span class="e-translation">the oats were damaged by the hail</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to break into (a song or dance), to suddenly start singing (a song) or dancing (a dance)</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_2">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хватить.html>хвати́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">xvatítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хватать.html>хвата́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">impersonal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to suffice, to be sufficient / enough; to last out
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́того</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:хватить.html>хва́тит</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">étovo <b>xvátit</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">this will be sufficient / enough</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сегодня.html>сего́дня</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:хватить.html>хва́тит</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">na sevódnja <b>xvátit</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">that'll do for today!; let's call it a day</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>у</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>него́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:хватить.html>хвати́ло</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:мужество.html>му́жества</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:делать.html>де́лать</a> что́-либо)</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">u nevó <b>xvatílo</b> múžestva (délatʹ štó-libo)</i> ― <span class="e-translation">he had the courage (to do something)</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>ему́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:хватить.html>хвати́ло</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:время.html>вре́мени</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:делать.html>де́лать</a> что́-либо)</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">jemú <b>xvatílo</b> vrémeni (délatʹ štó-libo)</i> ― <span class="e-translation">he had (the) time enough</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́того</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:должный.html>должно́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:хватить.html>хвати́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:зима.html>зи́му</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">étovo dolžnó <b>xvatítʹ</b> ná zimu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">this must last the winter</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́того</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>ему́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:хватить.html>хва́тит</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:месяц.html>ме́сяц</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">étovo jemú <b>xvátit</b> na mésjac</i> ― <span class="e-translation">it will last him a month</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>мне</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:хватить.html>хва́тит</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">mne <b>xvátit</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">that's enough for me, that will do for me</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:хватить.html>хва́тит</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">ne <b>xvátit</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">not be enough</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:хватать.html>хвата́ет</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:время.html>вре́мени</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:для.html>для</a> кого́-либо / чего́-либо; <a href = vnd.unilang:делать.html>де́лать</a> что́-либо)</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">ne <b>xvatájet</b> vrémeni (dlja kovó-libo / čevó-libo; délatʹ štó-libo)</i> ― <span class="e-translation">there isn't enough time (for something; to do something)</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>у</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>него́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:хватать.html>хвата́ет</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:время.html>вре́мени</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">u nevó ne <b>xvatájet</b> vrémeni</i> ― <span class="e-translation">he is hard pressed for time</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>у</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>него́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:хватать.html>хвата́ет</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:деньги.html>де́нег</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">u nevó ne <b>xvatájet</b> déneg</i> ― <span class="e-translation">he is short of money</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>у</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>него́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:шарик.html>ша́риков</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:хватать.html>хвата́ет</a></b></i> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">u nevó šárikov ne <b>xvatájet</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">he is not all there</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>ему́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:порох.html>по́роха</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:хватать.html>хвата́ет</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">jemú póroxa ne <b>xvatájet</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">he lacks the energy; he has not got it in him, he is not up to it</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:хватить.html>хва́тит</a></b>!</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>xvátit</b>!</i> ― <span class="e-translation">that will do!; enough of that!, enough!, stop it!</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>меня́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:хватить.html>хва́тит</a></b>!</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">s menjá <b>xvátit</b>!</i> ― <span class="e-translation">I have had enough!</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́того</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:еще.html>ещё</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:хватать.html>хвата́ло</a></b></i> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">étovo ješčó ne <b>xvatálo</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">that's a bit too thick, that's the limit, that would be the last straw</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***хватиться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:хватиться.html>хвати́ться</a> (13142)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хватить.html>хвати́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">xvatítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хватиться.html>хвати́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">xvatítʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хвататься.html>хвата́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to snatch <i>(at)</i>, to grip, to pluck <i>(at)</i>, to catch <i>(at)</i></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to miss, to notice the absence <i>(of)</i>, to find that smb/smth is missing
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:хватиться.html>хвати́ться</a></b> кого́-л</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>xvatítʹsja</b> kovó-l</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">to miss smb; notice smb's absence</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>его́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:хватиться.html>хвати́лись</a></b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:но.html>но</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>бы́ло</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:поздно.html>по́здно</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">jevó <b>xvatílisʹ</b>, no býlo pózdno</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">when they missed him, it was too late</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:когда.html>когда́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вы.html>вы</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:хватиться.html>хвати́лись</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:бумажник.html>бума́жника</a>?</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">kogdá vy <b>xvatílisʹ</b> bumážnika?</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">when did you first miss your wallet?</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to remember
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>я</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:слишком.html>сли́шком</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:поздно.html>по́здно</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:хватиться.html>хвати́лся</a></b></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">ja slíškom pózdno <b>xvatílsja</b></i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">I remembered [thought of] it too late</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хватить.html>хвати́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">xvatítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хватать.html>хвата́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">xvatátʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to grasp</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ка</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хватка.html>хва́тка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">xvátka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хватка.html>хва́тки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хватка.html>хва́тки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хватка.html>хва́ток</a></b>)

***хворост.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:рыжий.html>хворост</a> (12727)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Inherited from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">хворостъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">xvorostŭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*xvorstъ</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рыжий.html>хво́рост</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">xvórost</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хворост.html>хво́роста</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хворост.html>хво́росты</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хворост.html>хво́ростов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>brushwood</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">cooking</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> straws, twiglets (pastry)</li></ol>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*xvostъ</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хвост.html>хвост</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">xvost</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хвост.html>хвоста́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хвост.html>хвосты́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хвост.html>хвосто́в</a></b>)

<li>queue</li>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:хвостик.html>хво́стик</a> (8628)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хвост.html>хвост</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">xvost</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ик</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ik</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хвостик.html>хво́стик</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">xvóstik</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хвостик.html>хво́стика</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хвостик.html>хво́стики</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хвостик.html>хво́стиков</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">Diminutive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хвост.html>хвост</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">xvost</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span>: (small) tail</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> an additional amount
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>ему́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:пятьдесят.html>пятьдеся́т</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:год.html>лет</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:хвостик.html>хво́стиком</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">jemú pjatʹdesját let s <b>xvóstikom</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">he is on the shady side of fifty</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сто.html>сто</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:рубль.html>рубле́й</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:хвостик.html>хво́стиком</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">sto rubléj s <b>xvóstikom</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">one hundred roubles odd</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>squiggle (in writing), tail, end, hook (e.g. of the comma)</li>
<li>pigtail, ponytail</li></ol>

<table class="morfotable ru" style="float:right; clear:right; margin-left:0.5em; margin-bottom:0.5em; border: 1px solid 6699CC; border-collapse:collapse; max-width:300px;" cellpadding="3" rules="all">

<th ><a href = vnd.unilang:падеж.html>паде́ж</a>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хвост.html>хвост</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">xvost</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ово́й</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ovój</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хвостовой.html>хвостово́й</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">xvostovój</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> tail <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of an animal, airplane, etc.</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>; caudal
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:хвостовой.html>хвостово́й</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:отсек.html>отсе́к</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>xvostovój</b> otsék</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>tail</b> section</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:хвостовой.html>хвостово́й</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:плавник.html>плавни́к</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>xvostovój</b> plavník</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>caudal</b> fin, fluke <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of a whale</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***хер.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:хер.html>хер</a> (10393)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Originally <span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">Euphemistic form of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">хуй</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">xuj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хер.html>хер</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">xer</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr> or <abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хер.html>хе́ра</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хер.html>хера́</a><sup>*</sup></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хер.html>херы́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хер.html>херо́в</a></b>) <span class="ib-brac"><span class="qualifier-brac">(</span></span><span class="ib-content"><span class="qualifier-content">* See usage notes.</span></span><span class="ib-brac"><span class="qualifier-brac">)</span></span>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">vulgar<span class="ib-comma">,</span> slang</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> dick, cock</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">vulgar<span class="ib-comma">,</span> slang<span class="ib-comma">,</span> derogatory</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> dick, contemptible person</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li>When used in the expressions <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ни.html>ни</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:хер.html>хера́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ni xerá</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:до.html>до</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:хер.html>хера́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">do xerá</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, the last syllable should be stressed.</li>
<li>In the expressions <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:хер.html>хер</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ná xer</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:хер.html>херу</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pó xeru</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, the prepositions should be stressed.</li>
<li>It is sometimes considered a milder version or euphemism for <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">хуй</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">xuj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, especially in all vulgar idiomatic expressions, not necessarily involving the direct meaning "penis". E.g. "<a href = vnd.unilang:хер.html>хер</a>" is used more often in dubbing or subtitles than "хуй", to make phrases sound less crude or vulgar.</li></ul>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">хуй</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">xuj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Church_Slavonic" class="extiw" title="w:Old Church Slavonic">Old Church Slavonic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu">херъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">xerŭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, of uncertain origin: Possibilities include:
</p>
<ul><li>An abbreviation of <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Church_Slavonic" class="extiw" title="w:Old Church Slavonic">Old Church Slavonic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu">хероувимъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">xeruvimŭ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">cherubim</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">χερουβίμ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kheroubím</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Hebrew_language" class="extiw" title="w:Hebrew language">Hebrew</a></span> <i class="Hebr mention" lang="he">כְּרוּבִים</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="he-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kərūḇīm</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, plural of <i class="Hebr mention" lang="he">כְּרוּב</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="he-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kərūḇ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.</li>
<li>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">χαῖρε</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">khaîre</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">welcome</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.</li></ul>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хер.html>хер</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">xer</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хер.html>хе́ра</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хер.html>хера́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хер.html>херы́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хер.html>херо́в</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">archaic<span class="ib-comma">,</span> historical</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> the name of the letter Х, х</li></ol>
